# JOURNAL — shop-plus
Continuity ledger per CTO charter §6/§6bis. Every entry is evidence-grounded.

Format per entry:
## <date> · <slice/WO id> · <status: in-progress | in-review | done | blocked-on-founder>
- What was done (with the tool result / test output that proves it)
- Decisions made · safest-defaults applied on open ⏳ (flagged) · founder overrides
- Pending / next

---

## 2026-07-24 · OZ1 — BUYER-REAL-HONESTY-1 (what a real shop with nothing in it honestly looks like) · in-review — DO NOT MERGE
- **Why:** this is the slice that MUST merge before `VITE_STOREFRONT_BASE` is ever set. One coherent design pass, not four fixes: every item answers the same question. Founder ruled both design states; no fresh ruling was needed.
- **① FABRICATED TRUST — REMOVED.** `profile.ts` `httpStorefrontPort` returned `trust: {...AICHA_TRUST}` for EVERY real storefront — 16 deliveries, 4,8 stars, 12 reviews a real reseller never earned. Now returns the new `ABSENT_TRUST` (`{0, '', 0, demo:false}`). `demo:false` is deliberate: it is not demo data, it is the honest absence of history.
- **② BORROWED VOICE NOTES — REMOVED.** The same line returned `AICHA_VOICE_NOTES`, so a real reseller's product pages would have played ANOTHER RESELLER'S recorded voice as hers (worse than a fabricated number). Now `{}` — the existing, honest sans-voix state; no player, no gap.
- **③ NO-HISTORY STATE — « Nouvelle vendeuse »** (founder copy ruling; the plain form, NOT the warmer variant — trust territory is calm-and-precise, not Ouaga-warm). Rendered in `chips()` when `deliveredCount === 0 && reviewCount === 0`, as `data-role="chip-nouvelle"`. The two SYSTEM chips stay in every case — « Livraison Séra vérifiée & scellée » and « Paiement protégé » are platform PROMISES, not history the reseller earned. Catalog key `vit.nouvelle_vendeuse`, register `neutral` (matching its siblings `vit.ventes_livrees` / `vit.avis_verifies`).
- **④ NO-IMAGE STATE — the woven « SANS PHOTO » tile** (founder ruling, OPTION A). `tileArt` no longer reads `p.art`/`p.glyph` (VITRINE_SEED demo data a real product does not have); it emits a weave + C1's four corner ticks + the inline label. **THEME-DERIVED:** the weave is CSS over `var(--vt-accent)` / `--vt-soft` / `--vt-deep` (the cover-stripes woven vocabulary), so each of the four habillages draws its own and it works for a product carrying NO seed data. **LABELLED:** « SANS PHOTO » (founder: not « PHOTO À VENIR » — « à venir » is a promise the platform makes on the seller's behalf, and if she never adds a photo the platform lied; « sans photo » describes the state and promises nothing). Catalog key `vit.sans_photo`, register `neutral`.
  - **FOUNDER'S REFRAMING OF OPTION A, recorded because it is the durable reason:** A does NOT make item 4 live (real stores render zero tiles either way — see the gap below); it changes only the DEMO. The real reason is DIAGNOSTIC — if the demo kept pretty gradients while real products showed woven placeholders, device walks would keep showing something better than reality, the exact pattern that has burned this project repeatedly.
- **⑤ THE DEMO-CATALOGUE FILL — REMOVED.** `orderedProducts` appended `VITRINE_SEED.filter(p => !sf.curatedItems.includes(p.pid))` whenever no explicit pids were passed, so a real store whose curated pids are not demo-seed pids rendered the ENTIRE demo catalogue as hers. Masked ONLY because `flows.ts:92` routes zero-item stores to `renderVitrineEmpty` — it would have detonated the moment a real store had one product. Last armed instance of the pid-bug fabrication class that I know of.
- **Evidence:** typecheck **16/16** · tests **21/21** tasks, buyer-pwa **179/179** (+10 new in `buyer-real-honesty.test.ts`, +1 evolved in `reputation-render.test.ts`) · `run-gates.sh` **ALL GATES GREEN** · copy-lint **177 entries, 0 violations** · PWA payload budget OK · Playwright **32/32** · **frozen vault 0 diff** · money / seed catalog / `media/service.ts` / sandbox ribbon diff EMPTY · demo port data (AICHA_TRUST + AICHA_VOICE_NOTES) intact.
- **Screenshots (real code, no mock):** the four habillages shot from the built PWA through the Pages emulator (`weave-{laterite,danfani,indigo,foret}.png`) — each weave visibly distinct, ÉPUISÉ veil still composes. The « Nouvelle vendeuse » shot is the REAL `renderVitrineReady` output with `ABSENT_TRUST` dumped to HTML and shot (a first DOM-injected attempt was discarded as a mock — law 8).
- **Process note (my error, caught by me before commit):** a JSON round-trip on `catalog.json` converted six escaped ` ` sequences into RAW U+202F bytes (standing byte-scan law). Reverted and re-done as a surgical text insert: the catalog diff is now **+12 / −0**, all six escapes preserved, 0 raw U+202F.
- **NAMED GAP — REPORTED, NOT BUILT (founder order): the REAL-PRODUCT RENDER PATH.** The buyer vitrine cannot render a real product at ALL — not merely without an image, but no tile. Tiles come only from `sf.curatedItems` → `seedProduct(pid)` → `VITRINE_SEED.find`, so a real pid returns `undefined` and filters out at `render.ts`; there are ZERO references to `assetRefs` anywhere in buyer-pwa. **Scope of the missing slice:** (a) DATA SOURCE — a real listing has no producer on the buyer read path today; `GET /s/{slug}` returns the storefront envelope only (`StorefrontView` in `customer-projection.ts` carries `curatedItems` as bare pid strings and NO product records), so either that view grows a per-product projection or a second read route serves listings; the money law says the tile price must be HER signed price (`productSubtotal = B + M`), never recomputed on the buyer side. (b) TILE CONSTRUCTION — `tile()`/`featuredTile()` take `VitrineSeedProduct` (`pid,name,priceFcfa,inStock,art,glyph`); a real tile needs the same minus `art`/`glyph` (now unused by the renderer), so the seam is a `VitrineProduct` the seed maps onto — demo and real feeding one renderer. (c) ASSETREFS → TILE ART — canon v2.0.0 `SupplyProjection.assetRefs` is `readonly string[]` matching `CustomerProductView.assetRefs`; once boutik emits non-empty refs, `tileArt` takes the first ref as the tile image and falls back to THIS woven state when the array is empty (which is the normal case until boutik's media service is durable, R2-backed and deployed). **This is now on the critical path to the wiring flip and is nobody's slice yet.**
- **Also reported, not touched (possible fifth state, founder's call):** the C1 product page (`cliente/screens.ts:158-162`) renders a seed `productGlyph` under the caps label « PHOTO RÉELLE DU PRODUIT » and the caption « Photo réelle — ce que vous recevrez. » — i.e. the frame PROMISES a real photo while showing a demo glyph. Out of this slice's five items and inside the audited buyer flow, so untouched; it may want the same « SANS PHOTO » treatment.
- **Pending / next:** dispatch `ci.yml` at the pushed head → GREEN on-branch → propose guarded merge. **NO merge without approval.**

## 2026-07-24 · OZ1 — SUPPLY-DISPLAY-CONSUMER-1 (consume canon v2.0.0: productName + assetRefs on the supply wire) · done — MERGED at 5892734 (guarded: on-branch CI 30083368154 GREEN at head 5624647 · frozen vault byte-identical 521449…/09a649… · frozen-path diff empty · founder approval « approved and merge it »). NEXT: must land same-cycle as APPS's boutik producer migration to 642f849 — nothing deployed, so no runtime skew risk. Buyer no-image render state stays a recorded gap for a future buyer-surface slice.
- **What & why:** OZ1 is the CONSUMER half of the canon change (APPS owns the boutik producer). Canon merged `642f849` / **v2.0.0 MAJOR** — `SupplyProjectionSchema` now REQUIRES seven fields: the five economics + `productName` (`TrimmedNonEmptyString`) + `assetRefs` (`z.array(z.string().min(1))`; the ARRAY may be empty). The old five-field payload now FAILS the strict parse. Shop+'s `CustomerProductView` already declared `productName`/`assetRefs` with no source; the display data now travels on the existing supply wire, so those slots have one — no second read-model.
- **Re-pin (contracts + kernel-types → 642f849; i18n/ui-tokens untouched):** root `package.json` ×2, `pnpm-workspace.yaml` overrides ×2 (+ comment), `packages/supply-consumer/package.json` ×1. Lockstep is required, not tidy: `contracts@2.0.0` hard-deps `kernel-types@2.0.0`. Evidence: non-frozen `pnpm install` resolved `@platform/contracts 2.0.0` + `@platform/kernel-types 2.0.0`; lockfile now 28 refs at `642f849…`, **0** at the old `d7b27bb…`; `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile` → "Lockfile is up to date", byte-diff EMPTY. Installed `contracts@2.0.0` dist carries `AssetRefSchema` + the two fields (verified in `dist/shapes/commerce.js`).
- **Drift-check bumped 1.2.0 → 2.0.0** (`scripts/run-gates.sh`, both the positive and the tamper-negative invocations). It failed ONLY on the version arg (`pinned 1.2.0 ≠ manifest 2.0.0`); the 2.0.0 `docs.manifest.json` lists the SAME 11 docs shop-plus already carries (the new `docs/derivations/SUPPLY-DISPLAY-FIELDS.md` is NOT in the manifest), none of the 11 doc shas changed — so NO /docs sync was needed. `drift-check docs --pinned-version 2.0.0` → "OK: 11 canonical docs match manifest (packageVersion 2.0.0)".
- **Threaded the two fields (5 src + 2 tests):** `mock.ts` — `MockSupplyConfig` gains `productName` + `assetRefs` (both required) and the emitted value now carries all seven (a five-field emission would fail `.strict()` — the point). `opportunity.ts` — `customerSurfaceFromSupply` now reads `projection.productName` (the hand-passed `productName` param is GONE) and adds `assetRefs: [...projection.assetRefs]`; `CustomerSurfaceView` gains `readonly assetRefs: readonly string[]` (bare, matches `CustomerProductView.assetRefs` — ZERO transformation). `read-model.ts` — the stale "five-field" comment corrected to seven. `consumer.ts` / `index.ts` — NO change: the identity sweep regex matches neither `productName` nor `assetRefs`, and the projection type widens transitively (no hardcoded field list); not edited (no unrequested tidying).
- **Proved the parser accepts REAL output, not a fixture:** the mock's seven-field value flows through `consumeSupplyProjection` (the real parse path) → `fresh`, and the FRESH-PULL test now asserts `verdict.projection.productName` + `verdict.projection.assetRefs` survive the parse. Empty `assetRefs` = the honest normal case (asserted `[]`); a new `DISPLAY-FIELDS-CARRY` test proves a NON-empty `['asset/pv_img/cover', …]` also parses fresh and passes its refs through. The LEAK-KEY-SWEPT strict-reject fixture now carries all seven valid fields so its ONLY failure cause is the planted `supplierPhone` (honest assertion, not vacuous).
- **Empty assetRefs handled honestly; NO fabrication.** The consumer carries `[]` verbatim — never a demo photo, seed image, or `VITRINE_SEED` substitution (the pid-bug fabrication class the order named). The SW-2 LIVE no-supplier gate fixture regenerated with a single opaque, `productVersionId`-keyed ref (`asset/pv_o1/cover`) → gate GREEN (no banned key on the surface). `media/service.ts` validation, money paths, sandbox ribbon: UNTOUCHED.
- **Evidence:** typecheck **16/16** · tests **21/21** (supply-consumer **13/13**, +2 new) · `run-gates.sh` → **ALL GATES GREEN** (incl. the new SW-2 LIVE no-supplier gate + drift @ 2.0.0) · **frozen vault 0 diff** (`packages/commerce-core`, `services/attribution-service`) · money/sandbox/media diff EMPTY · diff = 11 files, +117/−67.
- **Open decisions (checked per §7):** OD-SDF-1 (rename/photo-swap propagation) **STAYS OPEN** — producer-side, "does not gate anything until suppliers rename"; not touched. OD-SDF-2 (version immutability) **ACCEPTED** — a future Boutik+ Build-Spec doc slice, not this one. Neither gates this re-pin.
- **GAPS reported, NOT filled (per the order):**
  1. **Buyer surface has no honest no-image render state.** `apps/buyer-pwa/src/vitrine/render.ts` renders every product tile's art from `VITRINE_SEED` glyphs/gradients (`tileArt` → `p.art` + `productGlyph`); there is NO `assetRefs`-driven image path and NO per-product « pas d'image » state — a tile ALWAYS shows a seed glyph. Wiring the buyer surface to real `assetRefs` (and designing the honest empty state) is a SEPARATE buyer-surface slice and likely needs a founder design ruling the way the no-history state did. Out of this slice's scope (packages/supply-consumer).
  2. **`category` stays UNSOURCED** — declared on `CustomerProductView`, deliberately not added by canon (scoped to name+images). Not filled opportunistically.
- **LAND TOGETHER with APPS's boutik producer migration to `642f849`.** A consumer on 2.0.0 against a producer on 1.2.0 (or vice-versa) fails the strict parse; nothing is deployed, so no runtime risk, but the founder must not leave the skew open across the two lanes.
- **Pending / next:** dispatch `ci.yml` at the pushed head → prove GREEN on-branch → propose guarded merge, sequenced with APPS. **NO merge without approval.**

## 2026-07-24 · OZ1 — SEAM-ERROR-VISIBILITY-1 (make the seam failure legible) · done — MERGED at 1651d88 (guarded: on-branch CI 30066464107 GREEN at the exact head 494c3b3 · frozen trees byte-identical 521449…/09a649… · frozen-path diff empty · founder approval « keep working and merge it »). Out of auditable candidates → make the failure legible instead of burning credits on elimination.

## 2026-07-24 · OZ1 — RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1 (the reseller app's first real writes to the live service) · done — MERGED at b5b65dd (guarded: on-branch CI 30062728647 GREEN at the exact head 928670e · frozen trees byte-identical 521449…/09a649… · frozen-path diff empty · founder approval, verified on the branch bytes)
- **CORRECTION accepted (founder) — the R2 "token" framing was wrong and inflated the risk:** `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN` is a DEPLOY-time credential (wrangler uploads the script + creates the `env.BUCKET` binding); at RUNTIME the Worker writes through `env.BUCKET`, a binding INJECTED by the Workers runtime with NO token involved. The deploy already listed `env.BUCKET (beurni-storefront-media)` live, so the binding exists — there is NO lurking token-permission failure. The only thing still unproven is narrower and lower-risk: that `env.BUCKET.put()` behaves against REAL R2 rather than miniflare's simulation. Use THIS framing in future reports, never "the token's R2 write is unexercised."
- **EXPO_PUBLIC_PROFILE:** the flag was the founder's (from a partial grep); the correction stands — unset ⇒ `IS_PREVIEW = true`, deliberately fail-safe. No code change.
- **NEXT SLICE — RESELLER-MEDIA-UPLOAD-1 (Option 1, founder; NOT started, after this merge):** add `expo-image-picker` pinned to the exact SDK-54-compatible version; wire a real COVER and AVATAR pick into K3 replacing the [DEMO] simulate; upload through the seam's existing `uploadCover/uploadAvatar` with `X-Write-Key`. **REPORT BEFORE BUILDING if the K3 rewrite turns out larger than it looks** (it is an audited flow — the founder wants that early, not bundled). `media/service.ts` validation STAYS UNTOUCHED: the 5 MB cap, magic-byte sniff and dimension bounds already run SERVER-SIDE before anything reaches R2 — the app must NOT duplicate or pre-empt them.
- **SEQUENCE (founder, unchanged):** ① RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1 (done) → ② RESELLER-MEDIA-UPLOAD-1 → ③ BUYER-REAL-HONESTY-1 → ④ the `VITE_STOREFRONT_BASE` wiring flip. BUYER-REAL-HONESTY-1 MUST merge before the flip.
- **Built (read-before-write: read collection.ts, customize/storefront.ts, storefront-core.ts, preview.ts, buyer profile.ts/render.ts/flows.ts, worker/* first):**
  - **Service — CORS on the READ routes only** (`src/index.ts`): exact-origin `https://beurni2.github.io` (never a wildcard) on `GET /s/{slug}`, `GET /media/{key}`, `/health` + an OPTIONS preflight; **NO CORS on any write route** (the reseller app is React Native, not a browser). Write gate untouched.
  - **Service — admin list** (`worker/storefront-do.ts` + `worker/index.ts`): a third ROLE of `StorefrontDO` at `idFromName('index')`, appended write-once on create like the slug pointer; `GET /storefronts` returns `{id,slug,name,discoverable}` with **live** discoverable (read off each entry, not a stale snapshot), **key-gated explicitly** at the composition root (a GET, so the write gate skips it — `keyAuthorized` extracted in auth.ts).
  - **Reseller seam** (`apps/reseller-app/src/vitrine/service.ts`, NEW): `StorefrontServicePort` — create/publish/unpublish/uploadCover/uploadAvatar/list — `HttpStorefrontService` (sends `X-Write-Key` from `EXPO_PUBLIC_STOREFRONT_WRITE_KEY`, base from `EXPO_PUBLIC_STOREFRONT_BASE`) · `DemoStorefrontService` (in-memory, zero network) · `resolveStorefrontService` (unset ⇒ demo, mock-gate by construction) · `deriveShortCode` (a valid `[A-Z]{2,12}-[0-9]{4}`). Results are honest `{ok:false}` on non-2xx / offline, never a throw.
  - **Env** (`expo-preview.yml`): the two `EXPO_PUBLIC_*` referenced as repo secrets so `eas update` inlines them; unset ⇒ demo.
  - **UI** (K1): « Mettre ma boutique en ligne » (create+publish) + « Voir mes boutiques en ligne » (list), wired from App.tsx via the seam; 7 i18n entries added (copy-lint clean). One stable session identity so a re-tap is idempotent.
- **Evidence (grounded):** storefront-service **66/66** (combined-worker e2e +4: exact-origin CORS on reads, preflight 204 without a key, NO CORS on the write route, admin list key-gated + live discoverable) · typecheck 0 both packages · reseller-app **240/240** (customize/journey/i18n-coverage green + new storefront-service.test **11/11**: demo substrate, HTTP request shape incl. `X-Write-Key`, honest failure results, resolver gate, deriveShortCode validity) · full `pnpm gates` GREEN (copy-lint, byte-scans, PWA budget, buyer Playwright 32/32) · frozen-vault diff **0** · **UNTOUCHED**: money paths, sandbox ribbon, `media/service.ts` validation, buyer PWA. **No listing writes anywhere.**
- **Founder decisions recorded:**
  - **CORS localhost (approved):** exact-origin only, **no dev-origin branch in production**. A LOCAL PWA build pointed at the live Worker WILL fail CORS until a dev origin is added deliberately — **known, accepted, NOT a bug**; do not debug it as one.
  - **Admin index — single directory object is correct here, not inconsistent with the slug decision** (founder): the slug index sits on the READ path and is touched by every buyer page view (hotspot → rejected as one object); the admin index is written ONLY on create and read ONLY by the founder — a different contention profile entirely. A single index object has a **size ceiling** (irrelevant at this scale, **not infinite**).
  - **Key in the published EAS-update bundle** (founder): easier to fetch than decompiling a binary — inside the shared-secret limitation already accepted; **reinforces the HARD GATE** (no reseller but the founder onboards until real per-reseller identity lands).
- **Findings REPORTED, not patched (founder's « report don't invent »):**
  - **EXPO_PUBLIC_PROFILE — CORRECTED, not confirmed:** it is intentionally never assigned; unset ⇒ `isPreviewProfile(undefined)` ⇒ `IS_PREVIEW = true`, so the preview signal FIRES by default (a production build would SET it to flip off). The JOURNAL's own fresh-context verifier already proved "unset → banner ON in the real bundle" (2026-07-22 entry). **No bug.**
  - **Empty-state (the two masked demo-fallbacks):** for THIS slice's case — a real storefront with `curatedItems: []` — the buyer PWA is HONEST: `flows.ts:92` routes it to `renderVitrineEmpty`, whose compact identity omits trust chips + delivered count (no demo products, no fake numbers). BUT two fallbacks are armed and masked ONLY by that empty-routing, detonating the moment the store is NON-empty (listings milestone): **(1)** `httpStorefrontPort` (profile.ts:214) hardcodes `AICHA_TRUST` (16 deliveries, 4,8★/12 avis) on ANY real store → fabricated social proof; **(2)** `orderedProducts` (render.ts:195) fills `missing` from the ENTIRE `VITRINE_SEED` → the whole demo catalog on a real store. Both → BUYER-REAL-HONESTY-1.
- **BUYER-REAL-HONESTY-1 — NEW SLICE, recorded, NOT started; MUST merge before VITE_STOREFRONT_BASE is ever set** (founder): a real storefront must carry **absent** trust and **absent** notes (never another reseller's), and the buyer must render a new merchant honestly — no fabricated counts, no borrowed voice, no demo products in an empty grid. **Founder ruling on the no-history state:** a merchant with no deliveries/ratings/reviews renders as **« nouvelle vendeuse »** — explicit, never blank space, never a borrowed count.
- **THE ONE DEFERRED PIECE, reported not filled — the real device media upload:** the seam's `uploadCover/uploadAvatar` are built + tested (request shape + demo), and the service R2 write→read is proven in miniflare — but getting REAL image bytes off the phone needs `expo-image-picker` (SDK-54 ≈ 17.x; works in Expo Go, **no dev build**) AND touches the pixel-audited K3 [DEMO] cover flow. Rather than guess an SDK-pinned dep version + rewrite an audited flow inside this already-large slice, it is reported for the founder's nod as the thin follow-on. **Consequence: the token's REAL R2 write permission is STILL unexercised** (item 2's stated unknown) — it proves out on the first real device upload; if it fails, it is a dashboard token fix, not code.
- **PROVEN-BY-TEST vs PROVEN-ONLY-ON-THE-PHONE (founder's boundary warning, stated plainly):** PROVEN by test — CORS headers on reads / preflight / no-CORS-on-writes, admin-list gating + live discoverable, the seam's request shape (`X-Write-Key`) + honest failures + the demo substrate, deriveShortCode. **UNPROVEN until the founder walks it** — the RN app actually reaching the live Worker (create/publish/list), a real browser accepting the cross-origin read, and the real token R2 write. Green CI implies none of these three.
- **VITE_STOREFRONT_BASE deliberately NOT wired** (item 6): the buyer PWA stays on the demo port until the founder has created + confirmed a real storefront. Flipping it later WILL make the demo link `/v/aicha-4821` stop resolving (she is `DEFAULT_STOREFRONT`, a source literal, not a real storefront) — correct, not a regression.
- **Pending / next:** dispatch ci.yml at head → prove GREEN on-branch → propose guarded merge. **NO merge without approval.**

## 2026-07-24 · OZ1 — SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1 (shared-secret write gate on the live storefront service) · done — MERGED at 3f11fb2 (guarded: on-branch CI 30057542233 GREEN at the exact head 88ed9f7 · frozen trees byte-identical 521449…/09a649… · frozen-path diff empty · founder approval, verified line-for-line incl. the OPTIONS-safe-method call)
- **Founder verification note (kept):** SAFE_METHODS covering GET/HEAD/**OPTIONS** means browser CORS preflights are never gated — the founder flagged this matters more than intended, and connected it to the CORS finding now folded into RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1 below.
- **AFTER MERGE (founder does this, secret FIRST then deploy):** set `STOREFRONT_WRITE_SECRET` in the Cloudflare dashboard (Workers & Pages → storefront-service → Settings → Variables and Secrets → add a *Secret*), THEN run storefront-deploy. Secret-first avoids the by-design 401 window.
- **DEPLOYED (run 30058743154, from main @ 39afa05, SUCCESS — the gate is LIVE):** new Version ID `4dd408d4-46e6-4835-8f50-19f7e1b2de7b`; upload 640.50 KiB (grew from 639.14 — auth.ts shipped); DO + R2 bindings intact. Founder set the secret in the dashboard (secret-first) then deployed. **Trusted-not-proven-from-here:** `wrangler deploy` does NOT echo dashboard-set secrets in its binding list (secrets persist separately, a deploy never wipes them), and the sandbox proxy denies `*.workers.dev` so the live 401 can't be probed here — the write-gate behavior is proven by the 11 e2e tests on this exact code, and the definitive LIVE proof (401 without key / 200 with) lands on the reseller app's first authenticated write (RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1). Reads remain open by design.
- **Closes the finding (I independently confirmed it, then the founder ruled):** storefront-service had NO auth — `POST /storefronts · /storefronts/:id/publish · /unpublish · /listings · /listings/:id/hide · /media/upload` were all reachable with no credential; `handleMediaUpload` reads `storefrontId` from a query param and checks neither ownership nor existence, so anyone with the URL could write media into ANY storefront's R2 path.
- **Design (read-before-write: read worker/index.ts, worker/storefront-do.ts, worker/listing-do.ts, src/index.ts first):** all six writes are POST and all funnel through the ONE deployed entry `worker/index.ts`. New `worker/auth.ts` gates there, BEFORE any dispatch — so the 401 fires before any DO/existence lookup and can never be an existence oracle. Gate rule: any non-safe method (not GET/HEAD/OPTIONS) needs the shared key in header **`X-Write-Key`**, compared **constant-time** (HMAC-SHA-256 over a per-call random key → fixed-32-byte XOR fold, leaks neither length nor content; WebCrypto works in workerd + Node 20). **Fail closed:** `secret.length>0 && match`, so an unset/empty `STOREFRONT_WRITE_SECRET` refuses every write. Reads pass straight through (buyers hold no key).
- **Secret hygiene:** `STOREFRONT_WRITE_SECRET` is read from env (a wrangler SECRET); NOT in `wrangler.toml [vars]` (repos are public); a comment in wrangler.toml says so and warns of the by-design 401 window before the secret is set. Tests configure a TEST secret explicitly via Miniflare `bindings`.
- **Evidence (grounded):** `pnpm typecheck` exit 0 (src + worker configs); storefront-service **62/62** tests, combined-worker e2e went **3→11** — a test per gated endpoint (401 without / success with), reads answer with no credential, wrong-key rejected like missing, the 401 body byte-identical for existing vs absent target (no oracle), and a second no-secret Worker refuses writes even WITH a header (fail-closed). Full `pnpm gates` GREEN (PWA budget, buyer-PWA Playwright 32/32, every negative fixture failed as required). Frozen-vault diff **0 lines**; money paths, sandbox ribbon, buyer PWA untouched. Changed files: `worker/auth.ts` (new), `worker/index.ts`, `wrangler.toml`, `test/combined-worker.e2e.test.ts`.
- **WHAT THIS DOES NOT PROTECT (founder ruling, stated plainly — not a footnote):** the key is inlined in the reseller app bundle (`EXPO_PUBLIC_*`); anyone who decompiles the app can read it. It stops scanners and casual abuse, NOT a determined attacker. And because the secret is SHARED, one reseller can write to another reseller's storefront. **HARD GATE: no reseller other than the founder onboards until real per-reseller identity lands** — a shared secret is safe only while the founder is the sole writer.
- **OUT OF SCOPE, journaled only:** rate limiting; and the live-only media read gate (already journaled under STOREFRONT-DEPLOY-1) — neither in this slice.
- **AFTER MERGE (founder, not code):** set `STOREFRONT_WRITE_SECRET` (Cloudflare dashboard → the Worker → Settings → Variables and Secrets → add a *Secret*; equivalently `wrangler secret put`), THEN redeploy the gate. Secret-first, or every write returns 401 by design in the window between. The reseller app (RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1) will send that same key as `X-Write-Key`.

- **Founder amended the next slice's scope (agreed — the reasoning is sound):** `RESELLER-WRITE-PATH-1` as I'd have scoped it ("create storefront, publish listing, upload cover") was WRONG on the listing. WHEN BUILT, REPORT-DON'T-INVENT: what the buyer PWA renders for a storefront with no curated items, whether that empty state is reachable + honest; if it falls back to demo products, flag it as the silent-fallback class (not patch around). Listing path returns once boutik publishes real offers over a real wire — grounded separately in boutik-plus, not this lane.
- **CORS — FOLDED INTO RESELLER-STOREFRONT-WRITE-1 (founder finding, not this slice, but it breaks the next milestone):** the service has ZERO CORS headers anywhere (grepped src/, worker/, the health module — no `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`). The buyer PWA is served from `beurni2.github.io`; `httpStorefrontPort` (profile.ts:206) fetches `${base}/s/{slug}` from the workers.dev origin — CROSS-ORIGIN. Without an allow-origin header the browser blocks the 200 response and the PWA falls to its not-found state. Why nothing caught it: the miniflare e2e calls the Worker directly, no browser, no `Origin` header — every test stays green while the real buyer surface is broken (same boundary-gap class as the deploy-bundle failure). **Scope to build (after auth deploys): (1)** CORS on the READ routes only — `GET /s/{slug}`, `GET /media/{key}`, `/health` return `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`. **REPORT PROPOSED ORIGINS BEFORE BUILDING** — the buyer PWA's GitHub Pages origin at minimum; state plainly whether proposing a wildcard and its cost. Anything other than an exact-origin allowlist is a FOUNDER DECISION. **(2)** NO CORS on the WRITE routes — the reseller app is React Native, not a browser, not subject to CORS; allowing browser origins to write would widen the surface the auth gate just closed. **(3)** Prove it at the boundary the e2e can't reach: a test asserting the allow-origin header for an `Origin`-bearing request, and a preflight `OPTIONS` returning the right headers WITHOUT hitting the write gate (OPTIONS is already a SAFE_METHOD, so the auth gate lets preflight through — verified in SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1).
- **BLOCKING GAP (flagged, not fabricated):** the founder says "SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1 is unchanged — keep building it exactly as written." **I have no SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1 work order** — verified absent from this thread, the continuity summary, AND the repo tree (`grep -rI SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH` → NONE). I cannot build "as written" what I never received. Requested the founder re-send it (or point to where it lives). Not guessing at a security-sensitive auth slice on the live service.
- **SECURITY FINDING that motivates SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1 (grounded in `worker/index.ts` + `src/index.ts`):** the now-LIVE write endpoints have NO authentication — `POST /storefronts` (+ `/storefronts/*`) routes straight into the DO; `POST /media/upload` goes straight to the upload handler; no key checked anywhere (only refs are the unused GCS bearer + DO "authority" doc comments). Anyone with the Worker URL can create storefronts / write R2 objects. Blast radius low TODAY (nothing valuable there; URL unpublished) but real — this is what SERVICE-WRITE-AUTH-1 must close before the reseller app writes.

## 2026-07-23 · OZ1 — STOREFRONT-DEPLOY-1 FIX (the deploy workflow was missing `pnpm build`) · done — MERGED at 568f33a (guarded: on-branch CI 30049442315 GREEN at the exact head 776c9c2 · frozen trees byte-identical 521449…/09a649… · frozen-path diff empty · founder approval on record, verified line-for-line)
- **What happened:** the first-ever deploy was attempted twice on `11ec2ad` — once by the founder (run 30048921907) and once by me at his instruction (run 30049163344). **Both failed at the same place, and NOT on Cloudflare:** the `bundle:worker:combined` step died with `✘ [ERROR] Could not resolve "@shop-plus/observability"` / `The module "./dist/index.js" was not found on the file system`. The deploy never reached `wrangler`, never touched the account token, never touched R2. So the R2-write-permission unknown is still untested — this was upstream of it.
- **Root cause (read-before-write; both workflows read in full):** `ci.yml:30` runs `pnpm build` before its gates, so by the time storefront-service's tests bundle the combined Worker (`pretest` hook), `@shop-plus/observability` has been compiled and its `exports → dist/index.js` exists. `storefront-deploy.yml` went straight from `pnpm install` to the bundle with **no build step** — so esbuild, inlining observability, could not resolve its `dist/index.js`. On-branch CI was green because CI never exercises the deploy workflow's bundle-without-build path — exactly the "green CI proves less than usual here" risk the founder flagged for this slice. His call was right.
- **Fix:** one line added to `storefront-deploy.yml` — `- run: pnpm build` between `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile` and the bundle, mirroring `ci.yml`. Nothing else changed (diff = the one step + its comment).
- **Proven, not asserted (local reproduction of the clean-runner condition):** stripped all 8 workspace `dist/` build outputs → `bundle:worker:combined` **failed, exit 1**, with the identical esbuild error; ran `pnpm build` (turbo, 10/10 tasks, exit 0) → same bundle **succeeded, exit 0**, producing `dist/worker/worker.mjs` (606 567 bytes) — the exact artifact `wrangler deploy` uploads.
- **Scope guard:** only `.github/workflows/storefront-deploy.yml` is a tracked change; frozen-vault diff (commerce-core, attribution-service) = 0 lines; rebuilt `dist/` is gitignored, not committed; wrangler.toml still correctly marked UNPROVEN (the deploy still has not succeeded).
- **FOUNDER CORRECTION (verify next iteration, then use):** a `workflow_dispatch` deploy does NOT always run the workflow file from `main`. Once the workflow exists on the default branch — which it now does — you can dispatch it against ANY branch and GitHub runs *that branch's* copy. So the NEXT deploy fix can be proven on-branch before merging, instead of merging each attempt to main. To be confirmed empirically on the next round; if it holds, use it — deploy debugging usually takes several rounds and this keeps main clean. (This first re-run still goes from `main`, since the fix is now there.)
- **DURABLE FIX — RECORD, DO NOT SLICE NOW (founder, while the deploy is mid-flight):** the missing `pnpm build` line was the symptom, not the disease. The real fragility: `bundle:worker:combined` depends on the workspace being built and *nothing declares that dependency* — it works locally only because a dev tree always has `dist/`. Any future workflow that bundles without building fails identically. The durable fix is to make the bundle script itself depend on the build (e.g. a `prebundle`/`prebundle:worker:combined` build hook, or the bundle depending on `pnpm build`), so the dependency is expressed once in the script, not re-remembered in every workflow. Deferred by founder ruling until the deploy is proven out — do not spend on it now.
- **Pending / next:** re-run storefront-deploy from `main`; report whether the DO migration applied + both classes (StorefrontDO, ListingDO) were created, whether R2 accepted a write, and the Worker URL if one exists. Then HOLD — do NOT wire VITE_STOREFRONT_BASE or MEDIA_PUBLIC_BASE without approval (founder must see the deploy prove out first). A first-deploy R2 permission failure is EXPECTED (token has only ever created the bucket) and is a dashboard token fix, not a code change.

## 2026-07-21 · BUG 2 — the /v/{slug} deploy 404, reproduced against the real Pages structure & fixed · in-review (built + gates green on-branch; NO merge)
- **Order:** the storefront `/v/{slug}` nav STILL 404s on the founder's device despite a7381cf's vitrineHref fix. Reproduce against the ACTUAL Pages deploy (not unit tests); make vite base / 404.html / deployBaseFromPath / vitrineHref / manifest ALL agree with the real structure; add an e2e driving the real deep-link against the deployed base. Report the deploy URL + the exact mismatch.
- **Deploy URL (grounded):** no CNAME → GitHub **project pages** → **`https://beurni2.github.io/shop-plus/`** (one-segment sub-path `/shop-plus/`, which is exactly `pathSegmentsToKeep=1` in 404.html).
- **THE MISMATCH (three compounding defects, all real):**
  1. **vite base `'./'` (relative) × the SPA restore.** On a deep link Pages serves `404.html` → it redirects to `/shop-plus/?/v/{slug}` → `index.html`'s restore script `replaceState`s to `/shop-plus/v/{slug}`, which moves `document.baseURI` to `/shop-plus/v/`. The **relative** module script `./assets/index-*.js` (vite rebased it relative under base `'./'`) then resolves to `/shop-plus/v/assets/*` → **404 → the app never boots.** (This is the a7381cf blind spot: vitrineHref was correct; the ASSET resolution after restore was not.)
  2. **The deploy redirect-wrapper clobbered the restore.** pwa-preview renamed `index.html`→`app.html` and wrote a fresh `index.html` that meta-refreshed to `app.html?demo-journey=produit`. But the 404.html sends every deep link to `/shop-plus/?/…` → `index.html` = **that wrapper**, which discarded the `?/v/…` restore query and forced its own landing — so **no deep link ever restored**, independent of defect 1. (And the target `?demo-journey` was the route I just retired.)
  3. **manifest at absolute-root `/manifest.webmanifest`** (404.html link) — wrong host path on the sub-path deploy.
- **FIX (built):**
  1. `index.html` restore script **pins a `<base href="{app-root}">`** (`location.pathname`, e.g. `/shop-plus/`) BEFORE the `replaceState`, so `./assets/*` always resolve to the app root regardless of the restored deep path. Keeps vite base `'./'` — no preview/e2e churn, portable to any deploy path. No-op on normal loads (no `?/`).
  2. pwa-preview **ships `dist` AS-IS** (removed the redirect-wrapper step) — the deployed `index.html` is the real app (with the restore script), so `/shop-plus/?/…` restores correctly. The deployed root is the app's real root (S3 DÉCOUVERTE).
  3. manifest consistency: `public/404.html` link → `/shop-plus/manifest.webmanifest`; `public/manifest.webmanifest` gains `id`+`start_url`+`scope` = `/shop-plus/`. `deployBaseFromPath`/`vitrineHref` were already correct (dynamic base from pathname → `/shop-plus`) and now AGREE.
- **REPRODUCED + PROVEN (the founder's ask — a real Pages e2e):** NEW `scripts/pages-emulator.mjs` (project sub-path + serve-file-else-404.html, the behaviour vite preview cannot reproduce) wired as a second Playwright webServer (:4174). NEW `e2e/deploy-base.spec.ts` (3 tests, GREEN): bare origin → `/shop-plus/` redirect; **`/shop-plus/v/aicha-4821` deep link BOOTS the vitrine** (404 → restore → `<base>`-pin → assets load, asserting **zero `.js/.css/.woff2` 404s during boot** — non-vacuous: the old code 404s the module script here); `/shop-plus/s/aicha-4821?pid=p2` boots the achat S1 for the real product (Pagne wax). URL restored to the canon `/v/…` / `/s/…`.
- **Evidence (this session):** tsc exit 0 · vitest **12 files / 106 tests** green · Playwright **22/22** (incl. the 3 deployed-base) · `run-gates.sh` **ALL GATES GREEN** exit 0 · emulator smoke-tested (`/shop-plus/`→200, deep link→404.html).
- Pending / next: dispatch ci.yml on-branch, prove GREEN at head. **NO merge** per order.

## 2026-07-10 · WO-2.3 · E2 checkout failure paths — in-review (built + verified on `e2/wo-2.3`; do NOT merge — founder's reviewer decides; founder-authorized app-lane exception, this chat)
- No failures to report, every figure log-copied: tests **113/113** (66 commerce-core + 14 attribution + 8 buyer-pwa + 8 reseller-app + 6 discovery + 5 storefront + 3+3 obs/flags), typecheck 11/11, **"ALL GATES GREEN (positives passed; every negative fixture failed as required)"** incl. the seven new E2 gate invocations, Playwright **4/4** (two new bounding-box prominence tests), cold proof green from committed bytes.
- **PRE-FLIGHT (pin bump to canon v0.5.0 `0ff6696`):** all @platform/* pins + overrides + lockfile (regenerated, https-normalized: 27 scp-form → 0); ORDER_STATUSES import proof shows the EIGHT-member enum live at the pin; drift pinned-version 0.5.0 (doc bytes unchanged). **Integration cost surfaced by the bump, adapted:** `EscrowTxn.status` was a bare string carrying the LEG status ('held') — under the v0.5.0 aggregator-flow enum the txn stage is `'hold'` (legs keep provider truth); the happy gate fixture regenerated via the sanctioned `--write-fixture`; the funded-legs NEGATIVE fixture's txn status aligned so it keeps failing for the RIGHT reason (short+refunded leg, output log-copied). SP3.2 funded-legs gate re-proven at the new enum.
- **1. Payment-fail recovery (Contract E2 scenario #1):** `spine.failPayment` → canonical `payment_failed` (reason recorded: charge_rejected/charge_timeout/webhook_never_arrived — LOCAL knowledge; no canon payment-failure event exists, the webhook that never came is not an event). **The release is the rule:** new `release` reservation command — immediate (no TTL wait), reason-carrying, idempotent, refuses on confirmed (un-confirming is E3); the committed DO worker bundle rebuilt. **The alert is the net:** `reservationReconciliationAlert` emits `reconciliation.alert.v1` (payload `reservation_held_after_payment_failure` — Contract §6 verbatim condition) iff a reservation survives the failure; null on a clean world. Gate + negative: held-after-fail fixture with no alert → exit 1 (log-copied). Buyer PWA shows the honest state: « Le paiement n'est pas passé. / Votre argent n'a pas été débité. » with retry/abandon at EQUAL prominence.
- **2. Cancellation:** pre-payment arms (reserved · payment_pending · payment_failed-abandon) → `cancelled` + release; **post-payment REFUSES CLOSED** with the machine reason `refund_required_e3` and money records byte-untouched (asserted); buyer copy honest about the path existing later (« notre équipe s'occupe du remboursement ») — no dead end. `refunded` is UNREACHABLE at E2 (asserted).
- **3. Problem path (M4 "problem path equal"):** `ProblemReportBook` — structured records on the canon §6.4 reason codes (unknown code refused), `incident.opened.v1`, idempotent; **never moves money** (obligations/escrow byte-identical after a report, asserted; `problem-path-never-releases` scan gate + planted negative). **Equal prominence is tested three ways:** the `ORDER_ACTION_SURFACE` descriptor pins one weight class for both pairs; the component test asserts identical class attributes, one shared row, no `primary` split; Playwright asserts real rendered bounding-box height parity (≤1px) in Chromium.
- **4. Attribution collisions (SP-I01 first-lock-wins):** `AttributionLockBook` — first qualified token locks (`attribution.locked.v1`); a second VALID token on a locked checkout REFUSES (`attribution_already_locked`), the lock NEVER moves, `reconciliation.alert.v1` collision alert emitted, honest buyer message (`attribution.collision` catalog key); same-token replay idempotent. Gate replays the timeline through the REAL book; the re-attribution negative fixture (claiming the lock moved) → exit 1.

## 2026-07-11 · CI INCIDENT #3 (expo-preview red on its first armed runs) · fixed on main `21400d0`
- **Both armed `expo-preview` runs were red** (this repo ×2; boutik ×4, sera ×2 — one shared defect). Diagnosis from the complete Actions logs (pulled via API, log-copied): token check, checkout, install, `eas init --non-interactive --force` (`✔ Project successfully linked (ID: 3436dab2-922f-4f80-beeb-e17e85f1f099)`) and `update:configure` (`✔ Configured updates.url`) all PASSED — the failure is the third command's bundling: `SyntaxError: index.ts: Cannot find module 'babel-preset-expo'`, identical across the three repos. The token and the founder's account are NOT the cause.
- **Root cause (config-class, reproduced in boutik's cold clone, byte-identical error):** `babel.config.js` names `babel-preset-expo`; the app manifest never declared it; pnpm strict isolation leaves it unresolvable from the app directory on a fresh install; babel has no fallback (direct `@babel/core` transform emulation).
- **Why WO-4.0's evidence missed it (failure-mode #8, named):** the `expo start --offline` boot probe transforms nothing until a client connects, and local exports silently reused Metro's cross-directory content-hash cache (`$TMPDIR/metro-cache`), bypassing babel. Standing lesson: bundling evidence = a cache-isolated `expo export`, never a dev-server boot line.
- **Fix `21400d0`:** `babel-preset-expo ~13.2.5` (expo 53.0.27's own declared range) added to `apps/reseller-app` devDependencies; lockfile by regeneration (+3 lines, zero new packages, dup-key assert 0). Evidence: resolve-from-app-dir OK · gates exit 0 (ALL GATES GREEN) · cache-isolated export exit 0 (579 modules bundled) · boutik cold-clone proof of the identical fix passed.
- **The founder's next expo-preview runs are the only closure** — this entry claims the local reproduction and fix, never the publish.

## 2026-07-12 · WO-5.1 (the Grand Teint SUBSTRATE — incl. THE COLD-START PROOF, on the web) · in review — branch `e5/wo-5.1`
- **Why this slice exists:** de-risk the async-font cold-start risk. No screens, no kit rebuild, no token consumption. Anchoring: branch off main `7779964` (WO-4.2E done; local==origin). shop-plus carries BOTH surfaces — the RN reseller substrate AND the genuine web measurement.
- **design-reference/grand-teint/** committed BYTE-EXACT (55 files, `diff -rq` clean; sha256 table in the packet). Archivo (OFL 1.1) sourced + subset in-sandbox (fontTools 4.63.0 + brotli; provenance in `apps/reseller-app/assets/fonts/BUILD.md`).
- **THE TYPEFACE — measured, budget NOT busted:**
  - **buyer-pwa (web) — Archivo Latin VARIABLE woff2, wght 400-900: 30,352 B compressed** (the whole family, one file) — under the design's 65-80 KB estimate; the product first-load stays **12,248 B** because the font is a SEPARATE asset, not consumed yet (payload gate green). When consumed the total is ~42 KB, ~14 % of the 300 KB gate.
  - **reseller-app (RN) — static set 400/500/700/800/900, Latin: 170,704 B = 166.7 KB per app** — inside the 180-240 KB estimate.
- **THE COLD-START PROOF — the genuine measurement lives here (web, where the sandbox can be honest):** `apps/buyer-pwa/e2e/font-cold-start.spec.ts` drives `public/font-check.html` (a measurement harness, NOT product — like the prototypes' review harness) under **Go-class CDP throttling (4× CPU + 3G: 1.5 Mbps / 300 ms RTT)** and proves: **(1)** `font-display: optional` NEVER blocks first paint — the price text has a measured box at the first frame in the fallback; **(2) CLS = 0** across the whole load — zero layout-shift entries (optional never swaps mid-page; and the fallback is metrics-matched to Archivo's own ascent 87.80 %/descent 21.00 %, so a swap would reflow nothing); **(3)** with the woff2 **blocked entirely**, the fallback still paints « 12 500 F » with information intact — **a blank-screen font path is impossible.** **Method limit, stated plainly:** this is headless Chromium as a STAND-IN for Android Go; the blocking/shift behaviour is device-INDEPENDENT (a property of `font-display` + metrics, proven here), but the absolute millisecond is not a real-device figure — that is the founder's phone. `src/fonts.css` is the @font-face substrate the product adopts next slice (unconsumed today; test-proven `main.ts` references no Archivo).
- **THE ICONS:** reseller-app — 26 react-native-svg components (`src/ui/icons.tsx`, currentColor, 20 dp, geometry byte-identity, 12,130 B). buyer-pwa — 26 inline SVG entries (`src/grand-teint-icons.ts`, currentColor, 11,589 B) — **named distinctly from the pre-existing WO-4.4 `src/icons.ts` (lock/scooter), which is byte-untouched** (I restored it after the generator first collided — caught by the build, fixed by rename).
- **THE TWO DEPS:** `react-native-svg 15.12.1` + `expo-haptics ~15.0.8` on reseller-app (SDK-54 bundled, registry-derived); nothing else (test-asserted).
- **⚠ one honest gap:** Archivo lacks U+202F (franc grouping thin space) — invisible from fallback, tabular digits unaffected; named for the next type slice.
- **Evidence at `631166f` (build `0496b99` + the ns0: fix round) (my own runs, logs kept):** tests **+14** (reseller grand-teint 8 · buyer-pwa grand-teint-web 6) · typecheck 0 · **ALL GATES GREEN** incl. the payload gate (12,248 B) AND the cold-start e2e · reseller dual export exit 0 ×2 — **Android 584 / iOS 586 modules, UNCHANGED vs WO-4.2R (+0: substrate unwired)** · **cold proof green** (fresh `--local` clone, frozen install 0, ALL GATES GREEN, payload identical 12,248 B).
- **The ns0: fix round (`631166f`) — a parallel build agent's find:** the shared generator's PWA branch serialized every glyph as `<ns0:path xmlns:ns0=…>` (via `ET.tostring`) — inline SVG a browser DOM would NOT render. Latent because boutik has no PWA module and my first web test asserted the `d="…"` substring, not element well-formedness. **Fix:** `ET.register_namespace('', SVG_NS)` → clean `<path>/<circle>/<rect>`; `grand-teint-icons.ts` regenerated (zero ns-prefix); the test strengthened to reject any `ns\d+:`/`xmlns:` and require real svg/path/circle/rect tags. RN output byte-identical (fix touches only the PWA branch). Build + cold-start e2e + payload gate all re-green; buyer-pwa tests 7/7. **This is exactly what a fresh-context reviewer is for — the defect my own test let through.**

## 2026-07-13 · WO-7.1 record correction — the shipped verifier verdict was session-authored, not verbatim (+ standing rule)
- **Founder question answered honestly: the `VERIFIER-VERDICT.md` in the first shipped packet (merge `253c5b0`) was NOT the verifier's verbatim text — it was a session-authored SUMMARY.** What was session-authored vs the verifier's, exactly:
  - **Session-authored (mine, not the verifier's):** the whole document's structure and wording were rewritten/condensed; the verifier's `file:line` citations were DROPPED (e.g. `resolution.ts:1037`, `:1045-1048`, `resolution.test.ts:1123/:1137/:1150/:1188/:1210`, `vitrine.test.ts:456/:492/:504`, `share-hub.test.ts:866/:891/:899/:914`, `main.ts:176`, `demo-store.test.ts:139`); and — the clearest breach — the two OBSERVATIONS had commentary inserted INTO them (« → Founder signed off. » and « → FIXED (commit 51867f6). »), which the verifier never wrote.
  - **Near-verbatim (the verifier's):** only the closing sentence (« No tests-that-assert-nothing found; no supplier/commission leak path found; … The slice holds against canon. ») and the bare pass counts survived close to the original.
- **CORRECTED (record only, no merge/source impact):** the verifier's VERBATIM testimony is now attached as **`_review/WO-7.1-VERIFIER-VERDICT-verbatim.md`** (only the transport HTML-escapes `&gt;`/`&amp;` restored to `>`/`&`); the review zip was rebuilt so its internal `VERIFIER-VERDICT.md` IS that verbatim copy, and the session commentary on the two observations moved to the packet **README** (« Verdict provenance »).
- **STANDING RULE (founder, journaled — binds every packet refresh, all lanes):** **a verifier verdict is COPIED, never rewritten.** It is testimony, not documentation. Session commentary about a refresh goes in the README or a clearly-marked header — NEVER inside the verdict's text. A summary of a verdict, if wanted, is a separate clearly-labelled file; the verdict file itself is always the verbatim original.

## 2026-07-14 · WO-FP-SHOP REBUILD — finding #1 FIXED (the display font now resolves) · branch `e7/wo-fp-shop`

Verified: Bricolage-ExtraBold internal now `Bricolage Grotesque`, Instrument-Bold internal now `Instrument Sans Bold` — both MATCH. Money+French coverage intact (« 11 500 F » incl. U+202F + U+2212 on all faces).

## 2026-07-16 · CI POST-MORTEM — main went red on merge; my verification gap; fixed at 481beed
- **FOUNDER CAUGHT IT:** the `ci` run on the merge (`#55`, main @ 4999d59) was RED while I reported green. My miss.
- **ROOT CAUSE:** the `no-emoji-in-chrome` gate (Grand Teint §8, `scripts/gates/no-emoji-in-chrome.mjs`) scans ALL `apps/` source — comments included — for pictographic ranges (`2600–27BF`, etc.). The « ⚑ » (U+2691) flag-marker I used in two comments (App.tsx shareVia block; collection.ts VITRINE-REAL-BACKING docstring) tripped it. It was the SOLE red gate — every money/custody/discovery/attribution/copy-lint/drift gate passed (positives OK, negatives fail-as-expected).
- **THE GAP (mine):** `ci.yml` runs only on `push: [main]`, `pull_request`, `workflow_dispatch` — NEVER on branch pushes. I was verifying the `expo-preview` publish, not `scripts/run-gates.sh`, and never dispatched `ci` on the branch. So the full gate suite never ran on my work until the merge. The collection.ts « ⚑ » had been there since the seam (increment 1) — branch CI would have been red the whole time had it run.
- **FIX (`481beed`):** replaced « ⚑ » → ASCII « FLAG » in both comments. Comment-only; zero behavior/money/UI change (byte-identical runtime to 4999d59).

### 2026-07-18 · addendum — CI cold-clone root cause (lockfile `resolution.repo` scheme-strip)
- **Branch ci #58/#59 failed at `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile`** (not a gate): `git clone github.com/beurni2/platform-contracts.git … does not exist` — a SCHEME-LESS clone URL. Cache MISS (new lockfile hash from the re-pin) forced a cold clone that exposed it; main/sera stay green because the pnpm store is cached on the old hash.
- **False lead (#59):** added a 4th CI insteadOf for the scheme-less form — still failed. pnpm's git fetcher does NOT take the clone URL from git insteadOf; it reads it from the lockfile's `resolution.repo` field.
- **ROOT CAUSE:** my lockfile was resolved in THIS sandbox, whose git config rewrites `https://github.com/` → the local proxy; pnpm wrote `resolution.repo: github.com/beurni2/platform-contracts.git` — **scheme-stripped**. My `git@`→`github.com/` normalization never touched it (no `git@` there). sera's working lockfile carries `repo: https://github.com/…`.
- **FIX:** restored the `https://` scheme on all 5 `resolution.repo` fields (certification, contracts, i18n, kernel-types, ui-tokens) so the lockfile byte-matches sera's proven cold-clone form; reverted the dead #59 ci.yml rule. Committed lockfile stays gate-clean (0 `git@`, lockfile-url-form green). Re-dispatching ci for the authoritative proof.
- **CI GREEN (authoritative):** branch `ci` run #60 @ `b53571f` — **success**, full suite (install → build → playwright 43/43 → every invariant gate, positives + negatives). Cold-clone now works (the repo-scheme fix); this run was a cache MISS that cloned and passed, proving the fix. Founder approved merge.

Reported, not built.

The reseller reducer NEVER emits `ready` (a Node test pins that no record/stop/publish/re-record sequence produces it). `ready` is buyer-visible/backend-stored only; the buyer's two demo notes (p1, p5) are seeded `ready` behind the sandbox « aperçu » ribbon.

## 2026-07-21 · STOREFRONT-MEDIA-BACKING — the through-a-service media backend (mock-gated) · DO NOT MERGE
- **Founder work order:** make cover/avatar/voice media actually persist, through-a-service (phone → storefront-service → GCS), with the moderation states real and the GCS client behind a swappable adapter; gate entirely against a mock store (no GCS, no creds).
- **GROUNDED (reported before writing) — the existing demo-fed media port shapes:** canon `StorefrontCoverSchema = { status: 'none'|'uploading'|'pending'|'live'|'error', url?: string }.strict()` (v1.1.0+, consumed verbatim); canon `StorefrontAvatarSchema = { mode: 'monogram'|'photo', url?: string }.strict()`; voice note = LOCAL shape (not canon) `{ status:'none'|'recording'|'recorded'|'pending'|'ready', url:string|null, durationMs }` keyed pid→note. Buyer reads them via `StorefrontProfilePort.resolve(slug) → { storefront, trust, notes }`; all three currently hardcoded in `buyer-pwa/src/vitrine/profile.ts` / `reseller-app/src/vitrine/customize/{storefront,voice}.ts`.
- **BUILT (storefront-service, presentation media only):** `src/media/media-store.ts` — the `MediaStore` port (`put(key,bytes,contentType)→{url}`) with `InMemoryMediaStore` (fake, CI/tests) + `GcsMediaStore` (real, GCS JSON upload REST over `fetch`, NO SDK dep → nothing in the lockfile) + `resolveMediaStore(env)` (real iff `STOREFRONT_GCS_BUCKET`+`STOREFRONT_GCS_TOKEN` present, else the fake — the mock-gate is by construction). `src/media/service.ts` — `StorefrontMediaService`: upload → validate (image: magic-byte type jpeg/png, byte cap, pure-JS PNG/JPEG dimensions, standard box; audio: magic-byte format, byte cap, client-declared duration cap) → store server-side → moderation. Cover + avatar `REQUIRES_REVIEW` → held `pending_review` (STORED-BUT-NOT-LIVE); voice → `live` on store. `approve`/`reject` move a held record; `buyerMedia()` projects LIVE records only onto the canon fields (held cover → `none`, held avatar → `monogram`, held voice → absent). `index.ts` — `POST /media/upload` endpoint (phone → service → store; returns the reseller view; the buyer projection strips non-live).
- **PROVEN against the mock (26/26 storefront-service):** upload→validate→store→URL round-trips (fake store holds the exact bytes) · wrong-type (magic-byte), over-byte-cap, over/under-dimension, bad-duration, missing-pid all rejected and NOT stored · held cover/avatar invisible to the buyer until `approve`, refused by `reject` · voice live-on-store, buyer-visible `ready` · `resolveMediaStore` returns the fake with no creds and only `GcsMediaStore` when the env supplies both. No `@google-cloud` in the lockfile; no credential anywhere.
- **CANON GAP (reported, NOT invented):** canon `StorefrontAvatarSchema` has NO moderation status (only `monogram|photo`), while `StorefrontCoverSchema` has `pending`. So an avatar photo « en vérification Séra » is held SERVICE-INTERNALLY (`pending_review`) and the canon avatar stays `monogram` until live — which is fine because the buyer only ever sees live. IF the design wants the buyer to render an « avatar en vérification » state (not fall back to monogram), canon avatar needs a moderation status mirroring cover's `pending`. Flagged for the founder; safest default (service-internal hold) applied meanwhile.
- **FLAG (named, env-gated production step — like GCS behind MediaStore):** the CI-gated build VALIDATES images to the standard box and rejects over-standard; server-side re-encode/downscale (« resize to a standard ») needs a native image lib (sharp) whose build script is blocked in this workspace, so it is the production hardening behind the same env boundary — the app's image picker resizes on device today. If you want the real server resize in CI, that's a sharp-build-enable decision.
- **FROZEN untouched:** money/custody/attribution — none touched; presentation media only (loi 5). Diff: `src/index.ts` (endpoint) + `test/health.test.ts` (async) modified; `src/media/{media-store,service}.ts` + `test/media.test.ts` new. dist gitignored.
- **EVIDENCE:** storefront-service `tsc`+`build` clean · vitest **26/26** (10 new media + health async) · full `run-gates.sh` **ALL GREEN** (0 GATE FAILED) · credential/`@google-cloud` scan clean.
- **STATE: BUILT · local green · dispatching ci on the branch · DO NOT MERGE (report head).**
